### [1] [LLM-Based Static Verification of Code Against Natural-Language Requirements: An Industrial Experience Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17926v1)
*Zhi Quan Zhou,Dave Towey,Tsong Yueh Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出两阶段LLM工作流，通过结构化中间表示将自然语言需求转化为可验证规则并检查代码，实现需求感知的静态分析，左移验证活动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统静态分析无法检测代码与自然语言需求之间的语义不匹配，软件测试依赖测试设计和运行时环境，需要更早、更自动化的验证方法。

Method: 两阶段LLM工作流：第一阶段AI规则挖掘器从自然语言需求中提取可验证规则并识别歧义等；第二阶段AI代码审计员根据规则检查代码，使用结构化中间表示减少幻觉。

Result: 在智能车辆网络安全案例中成功应用，实现了需求感知和语义感知的静态分析，无需编译执行即可左移验证活动。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的静态分析能有效验证代码与自然语言需求的一致性，补充软件测试，并解决测试预言问题。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地用于生成需求规格说明、设计文档、代码和测试用例。相比之下，一个更困难的保证问题受到的关注要少得多：静态验证实现的代码是否满足用自然语言编写的需求。传统的静态分析工具能有效检测编码缺陷和已知漏洞模式，但无法确定程序行为是否符合预期的业务逻辑。检测此类缺陷需要基于规格说明而非仅代码进行推理。软件测试可以暴露其中一些不匹配，但其有效性在很大程度上取决于测试设计、可执行工件和运行时环境。本文提出了一个基于LLM的两阶段工作流，用于在智能车辆网络安全案例研究中解决这一挑战。在第一阶段，基于AI的规则挖掘器从自然语言需求中提取可验证规则，同时明确识别歧义、自相矛盾和其他不可验证的陈述。在第二阶段，基于AI的代码审计员根据提取的规则检查实现证据。该工作流不是让单个LLM直接根据冗长的自然语言规格说明验证代码，而是引入结构化的中间表示以减少幻觉、输出可变性、有限的可解释性和上下文丢失。由此产生的方法是一种需求感知和语义感知的静态分析形式，补充了软件测试。通过在不要求编译、执行或运行时环境的情况下分析需求和源代码，该方法将验证和确认活动左移到开发生命周期的早期。这种基于LLM的静态分析也是解决测试预言问题的一种新方法。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate requirements specifications, design documents, code, and test cases. In contrast, much less attention has been given to a more difficult assurance problem: statically verifying whether implemented code satisfies requirements written in natural language. Conventional static analysis tools are effective at detecting coding defects and known vulnerability patterns, but they cannot determine whether program behavior matches intended business logic. Detecting such defects requires reasoning over the specification rather than the code alone. Software testing can expose some of these mismatches, but its effectiveness depends heavily on test design, executable artifacts, and runtime environments. This article presents a two-stage LLM-based workflow for addressing this challenge in an intelligent-vehicle cybersecurity case study. In the first stage, an AI-based rule miner extracts verifiable rules from natural-language requirements while explicitly identifying ambiguity, self-contradiction, and other non-verifiable statements. In the second stage, an AI-based code auditor checks implementation evidence against the extracted rules. Instead of asking a single LLM to directly verify code against lengthy natural-language specifications, the workflow introduces a structured intermediate representation to reduce hallucination, output variability, limited explainability, and context loss. The resulting approach is a requirement-aware and semantics-aware form of static analysis that complements software testing. By analyzing requirements and source code without requiring compilation, execution, or runtime environments, the method shifts verification and validation activities left in the development lifecycle. This LLM-based static analysis is also a new approach to addressing the test oracle problem.

</details>


### [2] [Contextualized Code Pretraining for Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17957v1)
*Chen Liu,Qingyuan Liang,Hanwen Zhang,Zeyu Sun,Yakun Zhang,Lu Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了上下文化代码预训练框架，通过集成调用上下文训练CallerGen模型，在CallerEval基准上显著优于同等规模模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码模型未充分利用调用上下文，导致在仓库环境中生成的代码无法平滑集成。

Method: 利用静态分析从真实仓库提取调用者-被调用者对，构建感知调用的预训练任务和基准，训练多尺寸的CallerGen模型。

Result: CallerGen在CallerEval上220M和0.5B模型分别达到16.58%和22.81% pass1，超越基线且与更大模型竞争。

Conclusion: 调用上下文对现实代码生成至关重要，上下文化预训练可有效提升模型性能。

中文摘要：随着代码生成在提高软件开发效率方面变得越来越重要，现代代码模型大多在具有自然语言描述的代码上进行训练和评估。在实际项目中，开发者通常会在有限的特定项目工件下实现缺失的函数，而本地的调用站点上下文在周围代码中已经可用。这种使用上下文提供了关于预期行为的可行提示，但现有模型并未明确优化以可靠地利用它，导致实现可能无法与仓库环境中的周围使用平滑集成。在这项工作中，我们提出了上下文化代码预训练，一种感知调用的框架，它将调用上下文整合到代码模型的训练和评估中。利用静态分析，我们从真实的代码仓库中自动提取大规模的调用者-被调用者对，构建预训练任务和基准，使生成条件基于调用上下文。我们训练了CallerGen，这是第一个使用感知调用目标预训练的代码模型，涵盖多个大小，并在CallerEval上进行评估，这是一个具有现实场景的新基准。实验表明，CallerGen优于同等规模的模型，并在两个基准测试中与更大的模型保持竞争力。我们的220M和0.5B模型在CallerEval上分别实现了16.58%和22.81%的pass1，超越了基线。这些结果凸显了在现实代码生成中调用上下文的重要性。

Original abstract: As code generation becomes increasingly central to improving software development efficiency, modern code models are largely trained and evaluated on code with natural-language descriptions. In real projects, developers often implement missing functions under limited project-specific artifacts, while the local call-site context is already available in the surrounding code. This usage context provides actionable cues about expected behavior, but existing models are not explicitly optimized to leverage it reliably, leading to implementations that may not integrate smoothly with surrounding usage in repository settings.
  In this work, we propose contextualized code pretraining, an invocation-aware framework that integrates calling context into both the training and evaluation of code models. Using static analysis, we automatically extract large-scale caller-callee pairs from real repositories to construct pretraining tasks and benchmarks that condition generation on the calling context. We train CallerGen, the first code models pretrained with invocation-aware objectives spanning multiple sizes, and evaluate them on CallerEval, a new benchmark featuring realistic scenarios. Experiments show that CallerGen outperforms comparable-scale models and remains competitive with larger ones across two benchmarks. Our 220M and 0.5B models achieve 16.58% and 22.81@% pass1, surpassing baselines on CallerEval. These results highlight the importance of calling context in realistic code generation.

</details>


### [3] [BLAgent: Agentic RAG for File-Level Bug Localization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17965v2)
*Md Afif Al Mamun,Gias Uddin*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BLAgent是一个智能体RAG框架，通过结构感知编码、双视角查询变换和两阶段重排序，在SWE-bench-Lite上实现78-86% Top-1准确率，成本降低18倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG管道依赖静态检索，缺乏推理能力，难以准确识别有缺陷代码，导致文件级错误定位成为瓶颈。

Method: 提出BLAgent，包含三个关键思想：路径增强AST分块的代码结构感知编码、双视角查询变换（结构+行为信号）、两阶段智能体重排序（符号检查+证据推理），采用有界推理策略限制候选文件范围。

Result: 在SWE-bench-Lite上，开源模型Top-1准确率>78%，闭源模型>86%，成本比最强基线低18倍以上；集成到APR框架后修复成功率提升25%。

Conclusion: BLAgent通过有界推理和智能体RAG设计，在文件级错误定位中实现了高精度和低成本，并有效提升了自动程序修复的效果。

中文摘要：错误定位仍然是基于大型语言模型的软件维护的一个关键瓶颈，其中准确识别有缺陷的代码对于调试、根因分析、分类和自动程序修复至关重要。文件级别的错误定位在层级定位和修复管道中尤为关键，因为错误的文件选择可能会传播到下游阶段，如函数级定位和补丁生成。虽然检索增强生成（RAG）为将大语言模型置于仓库上下文中提供了一种有前景的方式，但现有的RAG管道通常依赖于静态检索，并且缺乏准确识别有缺陷代码所需的推理能力。在这项工作中，我们提出了BLAgent，一种新颖的用于文件级错误定位的智能体RAG框架，它整合了三个关键思想：(i) 基于路径增强AST分块的代码结构感知仓库编码，(ii) 从错误报告中捕获结构和行为信号的双视角查询转换，以及(iii) 结合符号检查与证据推理的两阶段智能体重排序。与先前的基于图或多跳的智能体方法不同，BLAgent采用了一种有界推理策略，将基于大语言模型的检查和重排序限制在一个紧凑的、经过检索过滤的候选文件集合中，避免了开放式的仓库遍历。这种设计平衡了定位精度与计算成本。在SWE-bench-Lite上，BLAgent使用开源模型达到了超过78%的Top-1准确率，使用闭源模型达到了超过86%的Top-1准确率，同时比使用相同模型的最强基线便宜18倍以上。当集成到自动程序修复框架中时，BLAgent将端到端修复成功率提高了高达25%。

Original abstract: Bug localization remains a key bottleneck for large language model (LLM)-based software maintenance, where accurately identifying faulty code is essential for debugging, root cause analysis, triage, and automated program repair (APR). File-level bug localization is especially critical in hierarchical localization and repair pipelines, where incorrect file selection can propagate to downstream stages such as function-level localization and patch generation. While Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) offers a promising way to ground LLMs in repository context, existing RAG pipelines often rely on static retrieval and lack the reasoning needed to accurately identify faulty code. In this work, we present BLAgent, a novel agentic RAG framework for file-level bug localization that integrates three key ideas: (i) code structure-aware repository encoding with path-augmented AST-based chunking, (ii) dual-perspective query transformation that captures both structural and behavioral signals from bug reports, and (iii) two-phase agentic reranking that combines symbolic inspection with evidence-grounded reasoning. Unlike prior graph-based or multi-hop agentic approaches, BLAgent adopts a bounded reasoning strategy that limits LLM-based inspection and reranking to a compact, retrieval-filtered set of candidate files, avoiding open-ended repository traversal. This design balances localization accuracy with computational cost. On SWE-bench-Lite, BLAgent attains over 78% Top-1 accuracy with open-source models and over 86% with a closed-source model, while being over 18x cheaper than the strongest baseline using the same model. When integrated into an APR framework, BLAgent improves end-to-end repair success by up to 25%.

</details>


### [4] [Verify-Gated Completion as Admission Control in a Governed Multi-Agent Runtime: A Bounded Architecture Case Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17998v2)
*Hai-Duong Nguyen,Xuan-The Tran*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 验证门控模式通过只读验证器实现多智能体系统的完成控制，实验表明在有限条件下审计性和故障关闭有效，但任务级覆盖和泛化能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统复杂度增加，完成问题从生成性变为运行时控制问题，需要可审计的准入控制机制。

Method: 提出验证门控完成模式，代理提出完成但由只读验证器决定，并实现了一个有界参考实现，通过事件记录和分组化状态进行审计。

Result: 在实验数据中，调用事件验证成功率为99.5%，但大部分数据来自单一集群，任务级覆盖率不可计算；影子验证器规则一致性98.58%，阻塞精度0.39%，但仅作为建议。

Conclusion: 只读验证门加上分组化准入记录使完成决策可检查且故障关闭，但关于部署安全保障等更广泛的结论不在范围内。

中文摘要：随着多智能体系统从短期交互转向使用工具、具有专门角色和持久状态的工作流，完成问题从纯粹的生成问题变成了运行时控制问题。本篇预印本研究验证门控完成作为一种受治理的多智能体运行时的准入控制模式：智能体可以提出完成请求，但一个只读验证器决定该主张是否被接受。模糊或证据不足的情况以故障关闭的方式处理，而分组化状态和事件轨迹保留了审计路径。我们考察了一个有界的参考实现，并询问已发布的证据能够支持关于可审计的、验证门控完成的哪些结论。在已发布的验证完成切片中，已知结果的调用事件验证成功比例为1,791/1,800 = 99.5%。这是一个针对调用验证事件的会计度量，而非任务完成率、生产可靠性或基准测试成功率。任务级别的验证覆盖率不可计算；1,762/1,801行来自一个高容量报告集群；仅17个事件被分类为生产环境。一个影子政策/治理验证器评估显示规则一致性为1,526/1,548 = 98.58%，在安全通过预测中假成功率为0/1,526，阻塞精度为2/518 = 0.39%，因此它仍然是建议性的。证据支持一个狭窄的结论：在观察到的条件下，只读验证门加上分组化准入记录使得完成决策可检查且故障关闭。关于部署操作、安全保证、结果改进、任务级别覆盖率、恢复有效性或外部有效性的声明不在范围内。

Original abstract: As multi-agent systems move from short interactions to tool-using workflows with specialized roles and persistent state, completion becomes a runtime-control problem rather than a purely generative one. This preprint studies verify-gated completion as an admission-control pattern for governed multi-agent runtimes: agents may propose completion, but a read-only verifier decides whether the claim is admitted. Ambiguous or weakly evidenced cases resolve fail-closed, while packetized state and event traces preserve an audit path. We examine one bounded reference implementation and ask what the released evidence can support about auditable, verify-gated completion. In the released verify-completed slice, the known-outcome invoked-event verify success share was 1,791/1,800 = 99.5%. This is an accounting measure over invoked verification events, not a task-completion, production-reliability, or benchmark-success rate. Task-level verify coverage is not computable; 1,762/1,801 rows came from one high-volume reporting cluster; and only 17 events were production-classified. A shadow Policy/Governance Verifier evaluation showed 1,526/1,548 = 98.58% rule agreement, 0/1,526 false-success among safe-to-proceed predictions, and blocked precision of 2/518 = 0.39%, so it remains advisory. The evidence supports a narrow conclusion: under observed conditions, a read-only verify gate plus packetized admission records made completion decisions inspectable and fail-closed. Claims about deployed operation, safety guarantees, outcome gains, task-level coverage, recovery effectiveness, or external validity remain outside scope.

</details>


### [5] [ProcCtrlBench: Evaluating Process-Level Defects and Control Preservation in LLM Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20251v4)
*Jiawei He,Jie Jia,Chenbo Liu,Chaoyi Xue,Yapeng Song,Xikai Yang,Dong Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ProcCtrlBench是一个评估LLM编码代理执行过程质量的基准，通过过程证据和控制保留发现被结果评估忽略的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅评估最终结果，忽略执行过程中的缺陷，缺乏过程可见性。

Method: 构建了包含11种缺陷类型、4个类别的本体，标准化轨迹表示，并使用控制保留量化执行过程质量。

Result: 在200个案例上评估，显示出有用可靠性、更稳定语义，并揭示了被结果评估忽略的执行质量差异。

Conclusion: ProcCtrlBench能有效评估执行过程质量，弥补结果评估的不足。

中文摘要：现有的用于LLM编码代理的基准主要评估最终结果。虽然这有助于衡量整体能力，但这些指标提供的可见性有限，并且常常遗漏在执行过程中出现的缺陷。我们提出了ProcCtrlBench，一个用于LLM编码代理执行过程评估的基准。ProcCtrlBench将重复出现的执行缺陷组织成一个可复用的本体，涵盖4个类别的11种缺陷类型，并通过标准化的过程证据而非仅最终结果来评估代理轨迹。为了支持不同代理之间的比较，ProcCtrlBench将原始日志标准化为统一的轨迹表示，并基于过程层面的发现报告校准后的评分卡。此外，ProcCtrlBench使用控制保留（control preservation）作为量化执行过程质量的方法，捕捉执行是否保持可解释、可中断、可纠正、可逆，并在需要时能交还权限。我们在从三个基准（AndroidBench、TerminalBench和SWE-bench-Verified）中抽样的200个案例上评估了ProcCtrlBench。结果表明，ProcCtrlBench可以以有用的可靠性实例化，提供比直接阈值化更稳定的语义，并揭示出常规基于结果的评估常常忽视的执行质量上的有意义差异。

Original abstract: Existing benchmarks for LLM coding agents primarily evaluate final outcomes. While useful for measuring overall capability, these metrics provide limited visibility and often miss defects that arise during execution. We present ProcCtrlBench, a benchmark for execution-process evaluation in LLM coding agents. ProcCtrlBench organizes recurrent execution defects into a reusable ontology covering 11 defect types in 4 categories, and evaluates agent trajectories through standardized process evidence rather than final outcomes alone. To support comparison across heterogeneous agents, ProcCtrlBench standardizes raw logs into a unified trajectory representation and reports calibrated scorecards over process-level findings. In addition, ProcCtrlBench uses control preservation as a way to quantify execution-process quality, capturing whether execution remains interpretable, interruptible, correctable, reversible, and able to hand back authority when needed. We evaluate ProcCtrlBench on 200 cases sampled from three benchmarks: AndroidBench, TerminalBench, and SWE-bench-Verified. Results show that ProcCtrlBench can be instantiated with useful reliability, provides more stable semantics than direct thresholding, and reveals meaningful differences in execution quality that are often overlooked by conventional outcome-based evaluation.

</details>


### [6] [A-ProS: Towards Reliable Autonomous Programming Through Multi-Model Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18073v1)
*Anika Tabassum,Md Sifat Hossain,Md. Fahim Arefin,Tariqul Islam,Tarannum Shaila Zaman*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出A-ProS框架，结合多模型生成与调试，在竞赛编程中通过有状态迭代优化显著提升代码生成成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLMs利用执行反馈迭代改进代码的能力，竞赛编程因其严格需求成为理想试验台。

Method: 采用混合多模型反馈框架，将生成（GPT-4/5）与调试（Codestral-2508、Llama-3.3-70B、DeepSeek-R1）分离，进行2x3因子设计实验。

Result: GPT-5从39个提高到85-90个，GPT-4从15个提高到31-38个；有状态改进优于无状态8.5-10.6个百分点，减少重复失败3.5倍；比基线提升2倍。

Conclusion: 持久上下文和多模型反馈对可靠自主程序合成至关重要。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在自动化代码生成方面展现出巨大潜力，但它们利用执行反馈迭代优化解决方案的能力仍未被充分探索。竞赛编程为此研究提供了理想的试验平台，因为它需要端到端的算法推理、在严格计算约束下的精确实现以及通过严格评估达到完全功能正确性。在本文中，我们提出了A-ProS，一个自主AI代理，通过将解决方案生成与专门调试分离的混合多模型反馈框架来解决竞赛编程问题。A-ProS采用2x3因子设计，将基于ChatGPT的生成器（GPT-4和GPT-5）与三个调试批评者（Codestral-2508、Llama-3.3-70B和DeepSeek-R1）相结合。我们在来自ICPC世界总决赛（2011-2024）和Codeforces（评级1200-1800）的367个问题上评估了六种工作流。结果显示，GPT-5工作流从39个初始接受的解决方案经过三轮改进后提高到85-90个，而GPT-4从15个提高到31-38个。对47个问题的受控消融实验表明，有状态改进比无状态方法高出8.5-10.6个百分点，并将重复失败减少高达3.5倍。与基线代理循环相比，A-ProS实现了超过2倍的收益提升，凸显了持久上下文和多模型反馈对于可靠自主程序合成的重要性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate strong potential for automated code generation, yet their ability to iteratively refine solutions using execution feedback remains underexplored. Competitive programming offers an ideal testbed for this investigation, as it demands end-to-end algorithmic reasoning, precise implementation under strict computational constraints, and complete functional correctness with rigorous evaluation. In this paper, we present A-ProS, an autonomous AI agent that solves competitive programming problems through a hybrid multi-model feedback framework separating solution generation from specialized debugging. A-ProS combines ChatGPT-based generators (GPT-4 and GPT-5) with three debugging critics: Codestral-2508, Llama-3.3-70B, and DeepSeek-R1, under a 2 x 3 factorial design. We evaluate six workflows on 367 problems from ICPC World Finals (2011-2024) and Codeforces (rated 1200-1800). The results show that GPT-5 workflows improve from 39 initial accepted solutions to 85-90 after three refinement rounds, while GPT-4 improves from 15 to 31-38. A controlled ablation on 47 problems shows that stateful refinement outperforms stateless approaches by 8.5-10.6 percentage points and reduces repeated failures by up to 3.5x. Compared to baseline agent loops, A-ProS achieves over 2x greater gains, highlighting the importance of persistent context and multi-model feedback for reliable autonomous program synthesis.

</details>


### [7] [Three Heads Are Better Than One: A Multi-perspective Reasoning Framework for Enhanced Vulnerability Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18153v1)
*Xin Peng,Bo Lin,Jing Wang,Xiaoling Li,Jun Ma,Jie Yu,Xiaoguang Mao,Shangwen Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ReasonVul是一种多视角推理框架，通过三个LLM智能体的辩论机制，在漏洞检测中取得了显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有漏洞检测方法依赖单一推理范式，难以应对真实世界漏洞的复杂性，因此需要多视角推理框架。

Method: 提出ReasonVul框架，包含三个专业LLM智能体分别采用不同推理模式，先独立分析，再通过结构化辩论机制进行迭代反驳和修订，最终协作判断。

Result: 在PrimeVul数据集上，PairAcc为40.00%，F1为72.52%，PairAcc比最佳基线提升81.24%；在JITVUL数据集上PairAcc为28.67%。分析542个冲突案例，389个被正确解决。

Conclusion: 多视角推理和协作验证对于实现稳健全面的漏洞检测至关重要。

中文摘要：自动化漏洞检测对于增强软件安全性至关重要，它通过识别攻击者可能利用的潜在缺陷，从而减少对劳动密集型人工代码审计的依赖。最近的进展转向利用大型语言模型（LLM）进行漏洞检测，像Vul-RAG和VulnSage等技术通过结构化提示和外部知识集成展示了进展。然而，这些方法通常依赖于单一推理范式，限制了它们应对真实世界漏洞复杂多样性的能力。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了ReasonVul，一种新颖的多视角推理框架，利用三个专业LLM智能体之间的认知协同，每个智能体体现一种不同的推理模式。该框架从源代码的独立分析开始，然后通过结构化辩论机制解决冲突，通过迭代的反驳和修订，最终达成协作判断。在PrimeVul数据集上评估，ReasonVul达到了40.00%的PairAcc和72.52%的F1分数，在PairAcc上超过最佳基线81.24%。在JITVUL数据集上的进一步测试证实了其泛化能力，PairAcc为28.67%。此外，我们分析了542个冲突案例，发现389个被正确解决，突出了框架通过辩论驱动的纠错机制发现隐藏漏洞的能力。这项工作强调了多视角推理和协作验证在实现真实世界软件系统中稳健和全面漏洞检测中的重要性。

Original abstract: Automated vulnerability detection is crucial for enhancing software security by identifying potential flaws that attackers could exploit, thereby reducing the reliance on labor-intensive manual code audits. Recent advancements have shifted towards leveraging large language models (LLMs) for vulnerability detection, with techniques like Vul-RAG and VulnSage demonstrating progress through structured prompting and external knowledge integration. However, these approaches typically rely on a single reasoning paradigm, limiting their ability to address the complex and diverse nature of real-world vulnerabilities. To overcome these limitations, we propose ReasonVul, a novel multi-perspective reasoning framework that harnesses cognitive synergy among three specialized LLM agents, each embodying a distinct reasoning mode. The framework begins with independent analyses of the source code, followed by a structured debate mechanism to resolve conflicts through iterative rebuttal and revision, ultimately converging on a collaborative judgment. Evaluated on the PrimeVul dataset, ReasonVul achieves a PairAcc of 40.00% and an F1-score of 72.52%, surpassing the best baseline by 81.24% in PairAcc. Further tests on the JITVUL dataset confirm its generalizability, with a PairAcc of 28.67%. Additionally, we analyzed 542 conflict cases and found that 389 were correctly resolved, highlighting the framework's ability to uncover hidden vulnerabilities through the error-correction mechanism driven by the debate. This work emphasizes the importance of multi-perspective reasoning and collaborative validation in achieving robust and comprehensive vulnerability detection in real-world software systems.

### [8] [CommitDistill: A Lightweight Knowledge-Centric Memory Layer for Software Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18284v1)
*Divya Chukkapalli,Thejesh Avula,Aditya Aggarwal,Harsimran Singh,Amith Tallanki*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CommitDistill 从 git 历史中提取类型化知识单元，在预算约束下命中率优于 BM25，但 LLM 作为评判者未显示显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件仓库中的历史知识（提交消息、讨论等）未被有效重用，现有 LLM 代理记忆方法未针对此场景优化，需要一种轻量级、确定性的知识提取与检索方法。

Method: 使用确定性正则表达式从本地 git 日志中提取事实、技能、模式三类知识单元，通过 TF-IDF 检索器（沉默阈值 θ=2.5）进行查询。

Result: 有用精确度 0.525（Cohen's kappa=0.633），预算约束（256字符/查询）下命中率 0.750（BM25 0.333, git log --grep 0.083），提取 10k 提交耗时 <4 秒。

Conclusion: CommitDistill 提供了一种可信任、低开销的记忆基础，在预算受限场景下表现优异，但整体效果（LLM 评测）不显著优于简单基线。

中文摘要：软件仓库积累了大量的非结构化知识，如提交消息、拉取请求讨论和问题线程，但开发者和AI编码助手很少有效地重用这些历史记录。最近关于LLM代理的 typed-memory 架构的工作（MemGPT、生成代理和Yang等人的PlugMem模块）认为代理记忆应该是蒸馏后的、类型化的知识，而不是原始交互文本。我们将这一立场适应于软件仓库自身的git历史，在受约束的机制下：确定性、无依赖、仅本地、无嵌入。我们提出了CommitDistill，一个开源的Python原型，它使用确定性正则表达式将本地git历史挖掘为类型化的知识单元（事实、技能、模式），并通过带有校准沉默阈值（theta=2.5）的TF-IDF检索器呈现这些知识单元，该检索器在分布外查询时放弃回答。该工件是一个信任仪表化的记忆基础：确定性、无外部服务、可检查的纯JSON存储、可调放弃。一个针对五个公共仓库（涵盖Python、JavaScript、C和Java，25,000次提交，1,167个提取单元）的案例研究报告了有用精确度0.525，Cohen's kappa=0.633（基于40个双注释Python单元）。决定性发现是预算约束检索：在每查询256字符预算下，CommitDistill在12查询基准上达到0.750命中率，而BM25为0.333，git log --grep为0.083。在四项配对LLM作为评判者的评估中（n=200时间旅行bug修复，两个评判者），涵盖对照、CommitDistill、一个预算匹配的CD-Hybrid和BM25，没有条件在主要均值上产生统计上可检测的提升，且CD-Hybrid在头对头中与BM25无法区分。在笔记本电脑上提取10,000次提交在4秒内完成。本文附带了源代码、注释、基线和可重复性脚本。

Original abstract: Software repositories accumulate large amounts of unstructured knowledge in commit messages, pull-request discussions, and issue threads, but developers and AI coding assistants rarely reuse this history effectively. Recent work on typed-memory architectures for LLM agents (MemGPT, generative agents, and the PlugMem module of Yang et al.) argues that agent memory should be distilled, typed knowledge rather than raw interaction text. We adapt that stance to a software repository's own git history under a constrained regime: deterministic, dependency-free, local-only, no embeddings. We present CommitDistill, an open-source Python prototype that mines a local git history into typed knowledge units (Facts, Skills, Patterns) using deterministic regex and surfaces them through a TF-IDF retriever with a calibrated silence threshold (theta = 2.5) that abstains on out-of-distribution queries. The artefact is a trust-instrumented memory substrate: deterministic, no external service, inspectable plain-JSON store, tunable abstention. A case study on five public repositories spanning Python, JavaScript, C, and Java (25,000 commits, 1,167 extracted units) reports useful-precision 0.525 at Cohen's kappa = 0.633 on 40 dual-annotated Python units. The decisive finding is budget-constrained retrieval: at a 256-character per-query budget, CommitDistill reaches 0.750 hit-rate on a 12-query benchmark against BM25's 0.333 and git log --grep's 0.083. On a four-arm paired LLM-as-judge evaluation (n=200 time-travel bug-fixes, two judges) covering control, CommitDistill, a body-budget-matched CD-Hybrid, and BM25, no condition produces a statistically detectable lift over control on the headline mean and CD-Hybrid is indistinguishable from BM25 head-to-head. Extraction over 10,000 commits completes in under 4 seconds on a laptop. Source, annotations, baselines, and a reproducibility script accompany this paper.

</details>


### [9] [Same Signal, Different Semantics: A Cross-Framework Behavioral Analysis of Software Engineering Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18332v1)
*Wei Ma,Zhi Chen,Jingxu Gu,Tianling Li,Shangqing Liu,Lingxiao Jiang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM软件工程代理的行为规则在不同框架间往往不一致，甚至方向相反，框架效应远大于LLM效应，因此单一框架得出的行为结论需要跨配置验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有行为研究基于单一框架提取规则，但这些规则是否适用于不同架构的代理尚未验证，需要跨框架大规模测试。

Method: 在生态规模上收集64,380个SWE-bench运行，涉及43个框架126个代理配置，通过固定LLM或框架分离变量，测量每个配置的行为-结果效应并分析一致性。

Result: 框架更换导致行为差异巨大，多数特征在方向上存在分歧（如错误率效应正负各半），框架解释的方差（64%）远大于LLM（10%）。

Conclusion: 相同行为信号对不同配置意义相反，单一框架的行为发现需跨配置验证才能推广。

中文摘要：基于LLM的软件工程代理的行为研究提取了关于哪些轨迹形状与更高解决率相关的操作规则：测试步骤紧随代码修改、错误级联较短或轨迹紧凑。每条规则通常源自单一框架，并且其是否以符号和幅度转移到结构不同的代理设计尚未得到直接测试。我们在大规模生态系统中解决这一问题：来自43个框架的126个代理配置的64,380个SWE-bench运行，其中每个配置将一个LLM与一个提供工具和工作流的框架（例如SWE-Agent、OpenHands）配对。我们通过依次固定每一层来分离框架效应与LLM效应，然后测量每个配置的一个行为-结果效应，并检查这些效应是否一致。在固定LLM的同时更换框架会在每个动作特征中产生巨大的行为差异。在大多数信号上，配置不仅在幅度上不一致，而且在方向上也不一致。错误率是最清晰的案例：47个配置在错误率较低时解决了更多问题，而48个配置在错误率较高时解决了更多问题。来自先前SE文献的其他五个连续特征和七个二进制模式中的三个显示出类似的定向分歧。框架身份比LLM家族解释了更多的这种变异：对于平均轮次，框架解释了配置间变异的64%，而LLM仅解释了10%。这意味着相同可观测行为信号对于不同代理配置可能具有相反的含义。因此，任何单一框架的行为发现都应经过跨配置验证，才能声称具有普适性。

Original abstract: Behavioral studies of LLM-based software engineering agents extract operational rules about which trajectory shapes correlate with higher resolution rates: that a test step follows a code modification, that error cascades are short, or that trajectories are compact. Each rule is typically derived from a single framework, and whether it transfers, in sign as well as magnitude, to structurally different agent designs has not been directly tested.
  We address this at ecosystem scale: 64,380 SWE-bench runs from 126 agent configurations spanning 43 frameworks, where each configuration pairs an LLM with a framework (e.g., SWE-Agent, OpenHands) that supplies its tools and workflow. We separate framework effects from LLM effects by holding each layer fixed in turn, then measure one behavior-outcome effect per configuration and examine how those effects agree or disagree.
  Swapping the framework while the LLM is held fixed produces large behavioral differences in every action feature. On most signals, configurations disagree not merely in magnitude but in direction. Error rate is the cleanest case: 47 configurations resolve more issues when their error rate is lower, while 48 resolve more when it is higher. Five other continuous features and three of seven binary patterns from prior SE literature show similar directional disagreement. Framework identity accounts for more of this variation than LLM family: for mean turns, framework explains 64% of the between-configuration variance against the LLM's 10%.
  The implication is that the same observable behavioral signal can carry opposite meaning for different agent configurations. Behavioral findings from any single framework therefore warrant cross-configuration validation before being claimed as general.

</details>


### [10] [One Developer Is All You Need: A Case Study of an AI-Augmented One-Person Squad in a Brownfield Enterprise](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18461v2)
*Marcelo Vilas Boas,Gustavo Pinto,Edward Roberto Monteiro,Vinicius Fernandes Carida,Danilo Ribeiro*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 案例研究表明，一名工程师借助四个AI代理，以规范驱动开发方式完成了原本需四人团队的任务，成本降低85%以上，规范质量和机构知识是关键约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏关于如何在受监管企业环境中设计或评估单人团队的结构化证据，导致组织无法获得指导。

Method: 报告一个案例研究，一名高级工程师在规范驱动开发工作流下使用四个AI代理交付棕地产品计划。

Result: 工程师以一半时间完成任务，AI代码首次评审接受率90%，集成测试通过率100%，直接人员成本降低85%以上。

Conclusion: AI并非取代团队成员，而是倍增了经验丰富工程师的吞吐量，规范质量和机构知识是单人团队成功的制约因素。

中文摘要：AI工具正在使工程师能够吸收以前分布在跨职能团队中的角色，然而在受监管的企业环境中如何设计或评估这种单人团队，几乎没有结构化证据。缺乏这类证据意味着采用此模式的组织无法获得关于哪些设计决策使其可行以及哪些条件导致其崩溃的指导。我们报告了一个案例研究，其中一名高级工程师在规范驱动开发工作流下，由四个AI代理支持，交付了一项原本计划由四人团队完成的棕地产品计划，耗时减半，AI生成的代码首次评审接受率达90%，集成测试通过率全部通过，直接人员成本降低85%以上。结果表明，AI并非取代团队成员，而是倍增了留下的经验丰富工程师的吞吐量，使得规范质量和机构知识（而非模型能力）成为单人团队成功的制约因素。

Original abstract: AI tools are enabling engineers to absorb roles previously distributed across cross-functional squads, yet there is little structured evidence on how to design or evaluate such a one-person squad in a regulated enterprise setting. Without that evidence, organizations adopting this model lack guidance on which design decisions make it viable and which conditions cause it to break down. We report a case study in which a single staff engineer, supported by four AI agents under a Spec-Driven Development workflow, delivered a brownfield product initiative scoped for a four-person squad in half the planned time, with 90\% acceptance of AI-generated code on first review, full integration test pass rates, and an above-85\% reduction in direct staffing cost. The results indicate that AI does not replace team members it multiplies the throughput of the experienced engineer who remains, making specification quality and institutional knowledge, not model capability, the binding constraints on one-person squad success.

### [11] [Overeager Coding Agents: Measuring Out-of-Scope Actions on Benign Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18583v1)
*Yubin Qu,Ying Zhang,Yanjun Zhang,Gelei Deng,Yuekang Li,Leo Yu Zhang,Yi Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 编码代理在良性任务中可能表现出超出请求范围的过度热心行为，这是一个新的授权问题。作者构建了OverEager-Gen基准，通过行为梯度验证器确保场景区分能力，并测量了多个代理产品和基础模型上的过度热心率，发现删除同意声明会显著增加过度热心行为，且不同框架的过度热心率差异很大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码代理拥有高级权限，有时会执行超出用户请求的过度热心行为，这不同于已知的安全问题。现有基准因提示中明确声明授权范围而无法有效测量该行为，因此需要专门针对此问题的基准。

Method: 提出了OverEager-Gen基准，包括：（1）通过行为梯度验证器筛选场景；（2）使用双通道堆栈审计内部工具调用；（3）发布consent_kept和consent_stripped变体。基于此构建了OverEager-Bench，包含500个场景，在多个代理产品和基础模型上执行约7500次运行，并通过重新标注验证了标签一致性。

Result: 删除同意声明使每个基础模型上的过度热心率显著增加（差值11.9-17.2个百分点）。不同框架的过度热心率差异显著：宽松框架（Claude Code、Codex CLI、Gemini CLI）为5.4-27.7%，而ask-to-continue框架（OpenHands）仅为0.2-4.5%。框架内基础模型方差达15.9个百分点，表明对齐效果未完全通过权限门控传播。

Conclusion: 过度热心行为是编码代理中的一个重要授权问题，需要专门基准进行测量。当前框架的权限门控设计对过度热心率影响巨大，模型层对齐不足以完全解决问题。该工作为构建更安全的自主代理提供了评估方法和见解。

中文摘要：编码代理现在可以自主运行，拥有shell、文件和网络权限。当用户发出良性请求时，代理有时会超出要求：删除无关文件、清除过期的凭据备份或重写用户从未提及的配置。我们将这些范围扩展称为过度热心行为，这是一个与能力失败、提示注入或沙箱逃逸不同的授权问题。我们提出了OverEager-Gen，一个专门针对良性任务上过度热心行为的基准。构建它暴露了一个测量有效性问题：如果基准在提示中明确规定了授权范围，代理就会停止推断边界，转而匹配声明文本。在Claude Code上，仅删除同意声明就会使配对场景中的过度热心率从0.0%上升到17.1%（McNemar精确检验p=2.4×10^-4）。因此，OverEager-Gen通过行为梯度验证器在准入前认证每个场景的区分能力，通过双通道堆栈（PATH注入的shim加上每个代理的事件流）审计内部工具调用，并发布字节相同的consent_kept和consent_stripped变体。OverEager-Bench包含500个经过验证的场景和跨四个代理产品（Claude Code、OpenHands、Codex CLI、Gemini CLI）及六个基础模型的约7500次运行；50样本重新标注得到Cohen's kappa=0.73，规则判断召回率=1.00。删除同意声明使每个共享基础模型上的过度热心率倍增（差值在11.9到17.2个百分点之间）。框架轴主导效应大小：一个宽松集群（Claude Code、Codex CLI、Gemini CLI）的过度热心率为5.4-27.7%，而ask-to-continue框架（OpenHands）为0.2-4.5%（Fisher检验p≤10^-5）。框架内基础模型方差达到15.9个百分点，表明模型层对齐不能完全通过宽松的权限门控传播。

Original abstract: Coding agents now run autonomously with shell, file, and network privileges. When a user issues a benign request, the agent sometimes does more than asked: it deletes unrelated files, wipes a stale credentials backup, or rewrites configuration the user never mentioned. We call these scope expansions overeager actions, an authorization problem distinct from capability failures, prompt injection, or sandbox escapes.
  We present OverEager-Gen, a benchmark dedicated to overeager behavior on benign tasks. Building it surfaces a measurement-validity issue: if a benchmark spells out the authorized scope inside the prompt, the agent stops inferring boundaries and starts pattern-matching declaration text. On Claude Code, stripping the consent declaration alone raises the overeager rate from 0.0% to 17.1% on paired scenarios (McNemar exact p = 2.4 x 10^-4). OverEager-Gen therefore certifies each scenario's discriminative power before admission via a behavioral-gradient validator, audits internal tool calls through a dual-channel stack (PATH-injected shim plus per-agent event streams), and ships byte-identical consent_kept and consent_stripped variants.
  OverEager-Bench contains 500 validated scenarios and ~7,500 runs across four agent products (Claude Code, OpenHands, Codex CLI, Gemini CLI) and six base models; a 50-sample re-annotation gives Cohen's kappa = 0.73 and rule-judge recall = 1.00. Stripping consent multiplies the overeager rate on every shared base model (Delta in [11.9, 17.2] pp). The framework axis dominates effect size: a permissive cluster (Claude Code, Codex CLI, Gemini CLI) runs at 5.4-27.7% while the ask-to-continue framework (OpenHands) sits at 0.2-4.5% (Fisher p <= 10^-5). Within-framework base-model variance reaches 15.9 pp, indicating that model-layer alignment does not fully propagate through permissive permission gating.

</details>


### [12] [Reversa: A Reverse Documentation Engineering Framework for Converting Legacy Software into Operational Specifications for AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18684v1)
*Sanderson Oliveira de Macedo,Ronaldo Martins da Costa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Reversa框架，通过多代理管道将遗留软件转换为可追溯的操作规范，并在ATM迁移案例中展示了初步结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遗留系统中的业务规则、架构决策和操作异常通常隐含在代码和实践中，而语言模型驱动的编码代理需要可靠的上下文和正确性标准才能安全地修改系统。

Method: 设计了一个多代理管道框架Reversa，包含专门代理负责映射项目表面、分析模块、提取隐含规则、合成架构、编写单元级规范和审查声明，并强调可追溯性、置信度标记和保留空白。

Result: 在COBOL到Go的ATM迁移案例中，生成了517个声明、10个空白、53个Gherkin场景和9/11任务完成的重建计划，但最终对等验证未完成。

Conclusion: Reversa为将遗留软件转化为AI可用的操作规范提供了方法，但需要进一步评估；论文贡献在于提出框架、评估协议和初步案例研究，而非广泛的经验优越性。

中文摘要：遗留系统集中了业务规则、架构决策和操作异常，这些通常隐含在代码、数据、配置和维护实践中。与此同时，基于语言模型的编码代理依赖于可靠的上下文、正确性标准和行为契约，以较低风险修改真实系统。本文提出了Reversa，一个逆向文档工程框架，用于将遗留软件转换为AI代理可追溯的操作规范。Reversa将该过程组织为一个多代理管道：专门的代理映射项目表面、分析模块、提取隐含规则、综合架构、编写单元级规范并审查生成的声明。该提案强调三种机制：代码与规范之间的可追溯性、显式置信度标记以及为人工验证保留的空白。该框架作为一个Node.js CLI分发，跨多个代理引擎安装技能，并使用SHA-256清单在更新或卸载操作期间保留修改过的文件。除了架构描述外，我们报告了一个探索性案例研究，将ATM从COBOL迁移到Go，其中管道产生了517条按内部置信度索引分类的声明、10个已注册空白、53个Gherkin对等场景，以及一个重建计划，在盘点时11个任务中完成了9个。最终对等验证和切换未在本研究中完成。我们不主张广泛的经验优越性；我们相对于逆向工程、基于LLM的文档和软件代理的文献定位该贡献，并提出了一个包含覆盖率、可追溯性、置信度、效用和成本指标的评估协议。

Original abstract: Legacy systems concentrate business rules, architectural decisions, and operational exceptions that often remain implicit in code, data, configuration, and
  maintenance practices. At the same time, language-model-based coding agents depend on reliable context, correctness criteria, and behavioral contracts to
  modify real systems with lower risk. This paper presents Reversa, a reverse documentation engineering framework for converting legacy software into
  traceable operational specifications for AI agents. Reversa organizes this process as a multi-agent pipeline: specialized agents map the project surface,
  analyze modules, extract implicit rules, synthesize architecture, write unit-level specifications, and review generated claims. The proposal emphasizes
  three mechanisms: traceability between code and specification, explicit confidence marking, and preservation of gaps for human validation. The framework is
  distributed as a Node.js CLI, installs skills across multiple agent engines, and uses a SHA-256 manifest to preserve modified files during update or
  uninstall operations. In addition to the architectural description, we report an exploratory case study on migrating an ATM from COBOL to Go, in which the
  pipeline produced 517 claims classified by an internal confidence index, 10 registered gaps, 53 Gherkin parity scenarios, and a reconstruction plan with 9
  of 11 tasks completed at inventory time. Final parity validation and cutover were not completed in this study. We do not claim broad empirical superiority;
  we position the contribution with respect to the literature on reverse engineering, LLM-based documentation, and software agents, and propose an evaluation
  protocol with metrics for coverage, traceability, confidence, utility, and cost.

</details>


### [13] [Prompt Optimization for LLM Code Generation via Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19102v1)
*Ali Mohammadi Esfahani,Nafiseh Kahani,Samuel A. Ajila*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出基于PPO的强化学习框架，通过混合动作空间和单元测试驱动的塑形奖励自动优化提示，显著提升了LLM代码生成的功能正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代码生成对提示表述高度敏感，手动调优成本高且不稳定，因此需要自动化的提示优化方法。

Method: 将提示优化建模为序列决策问题，使用PPO代理通过混合动作空间（直接生成、遗传词汇突变、语义重写）迭代改进提示，以单元测试反馈的塑形奖励作为指导。

Result: 在MBPP+、HumanEval+和APPS上，使用CodeT5+、CodeLLaMA和DeepSeek-Coder作为代码生成器，PPO代理在严格Pass@1和Soft-Pass@1上均显著优于EPiC、Reflexion和Random-Hybrid基线。

Conclusion: 强化学习结合塑形测试驱动奖励能够有效提高LLM代码生成的功能正确性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够从自然语言生成代码，但其性能对提示（prompt）的表述非常敏感。我们提出一个基于强化学习的框架，将提示优化建模为序列决策问题。一个近端策略优化（PPO）代理通过混合动作空间（结合直接生成、遗传词汇突变和语义重写）迭代改进提示，并由源自单元测试反馈的塑形奖励引导。我们在MBPP+、HumanEval+和APPS上评估该框架，使用CodeT5+、CodeLLaMA和DeepSeek-Coder作为冻结的代码生成器。在500任务的MBPP+测试集上，PPO代理分别达到57.58%、64.80%和85.50%的严格Pass@1分数，优于EPiC、Reflexion和Random-Hybrid。Soft-Pass@1分别达到67.90%、73.10%和88.20%。在HumanEval+和APPS上，所有骨干模型均观察到类似改进。结果表明，使用塑形测试驱动奖励的强化学习提高了基于LLM的代码生成的功能正确性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate code from natural language, but their performance is highly sensitive to prompt formulation. We propose a reinforcement-learning-based framework that models prompt refinement as a sequential decision-making problem. A Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) agent iteratively improves prompts using a hybrid action space that combines direct generation, genetic lexical mutation and semantic rewriting, guided by shaped rewards derived from unit-test feedback. We evaluate the framework on MBPP+, HumanEval+, and APPS using CodeT5+, CodeLLaMA, and DeepSeek-Coder as frozen code generators. On the 500-task MBPP+ test set, the PPO agent achieves strict Pass@1 scores of 57.58%, 64.80%, and 85.50%, respectively, outperforming EPiC, Reflexion, and Random-Hybrid. Soft-Pass@1 reaches 67.90%, 73.10%, and 88.20%, respectively. Similar improvements are observed on HumanEval+ and APPS across all backbone models. The results demonstrate that reinforcement learning with shaped test-driven rewards improves functional correctness in LLM-based code generation.

</details>


### [14] [Restructure This: Using AI to Restructure Onboarding Documents to Reduce Cognitive Overload](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19174v2)
*Zixuan Feng,Prashant Tandan,Igor Steinmacher,Marco Aurelio Gerosa,Anita Sarma*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 利用CTML策略和GenAI管道重构OSS文档，降低新手认知负荷，提升任务成功率和可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OSS入门文档通常难以理解，导致新手认知过载和放弃，需要有效的重构方法。

Method: 基于CTML策略，使用GenAI管道开发VisDoc原型，将文档分割为任务单元、推断流程、去冗余并生成多模态解释。

Result: 专家评估确认了完整性和准确性；用户实验表明VisDoc显著降低认知负荷、提高任务成功率和感知可用性。

Conclusion: 认知信息型文档重构能有效降低认知负荷，提升OSS文档的可用性和任务绩效。

中文摘要：入门文档对于吸引和留住开源软件（OSS）的新手至关重要。然而，这些文档通常呈现为密集、结构不一致且碎片化的内容，难以理解，从而导致认知过载，进而引发挫败感、错误和放弃。本文研究了如何利用多媒体学习认知理论（CTML）策略来重构OSS文档。我们使用基于GenAI的流程来实施这些策略，通过原型VisDoc重构OSS文档。VisDoc将文档分割成基于任务的单元，推断工作流程，去除冗余，并生成多模态解释。一项专家评估（N=4）肯定了VisDoc的完整性、准确性和可采纳性；一项针对新手的被试间评估（N=14）发现，VisDoc参与者获得了更高的任务成功率，认知负荷显著降低，并且感知可用性更高。本文的贡献包括基于CTML的入门挑战分析、基于GenAI的文档重构流程，以及认知信息型文档重构可降低认知负荷、提高OSS中可用性和任务绩效的实证证据。

Original abstract: Onboarding documentation is critical for attracting and retaining newcomers in open source software (OSS). However, it is often presented as dense, inconsistently structured, and fragmented presentations that are difficult to understand, which creates cognitive overload leading to frustration, errors, and abandonment. Here, we investigate how Cognitive Theory of Multimedia Learning (CTML) strategies can be used to restructure OSS documentation. We use a GenAI-based pipeline to operationalize these strategies to restructure OSS documentation through our prototype VisDoc. VisDoc segments documentation into task-based units, infers workflows, removes redundancy, and generates multimodal explanations. An expert evaluation (N=4) affirmed VisDoc's completeness, accuracy, and adoptability; A between-subjects evaluation (N=14) with newcomers found that VisDoc participants achieved higher task success, had significantly lower cognitive load, and perceived higher usability. The contributions of this work include a CTML-grounded analysis of onboarding challenges, a GenAI-based documentation restructuring pipeline, and empirical evidence that cognitively informed documentation restructuring reduces cognitive load and improves usability and task performance in OSS.

</details>


### [15] [Supporting System Testing with a Multi-Agent LLM-based Framework for Knowledge Graph Extraction: A Case Study with Ethernet Switch Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19180v1)
*Rongqi Pan,Mahboubeh Dadkhah,Jean Baptiste Minani,Hussein Al Osman,Lionel Briand,Haiwei Dong*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个基于多智能体LLM的通用框架，从半结构化技术文档（如以太网交换机配置手册）中提取知识图谱，并通过迭代改进达到高正确性，进而支持下游测试用例生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 技术文档包含丰富领域知识，但其半结构化格式、隐式属性和复杂依赖关系使其难以直接用于测试自动化。

Method: 采用多智能体LLM框架，结合细粒度知识图谱模式和迭代的提取-评估-改进（EEI）循环，从ESCM中提取、评估并优化知识图谱。

Result: 在50个真实ESCM上，原始提示下平均正确性0.97-0.99；EEI循环进一步提升；LLM与人工评估一致性高（Cohen's kappa≥0.72）；工业测试人员反馈知识图谱可支持生成有用正确的测试用例规范。

Conclusion: 该通用框架可有效从半结构化工业文档中提取结构化知识，助力下游任务自动化。

中文摘要：技术文档包含丰富的领域知识，可用于自动化下游任务，例如系统测试。虽然本文聚焦于以太网交换机配置手册（ESCM），但我们提出了一个通用框架，可适应不同的工业场景。ESCM为以太网交换机测试提供了宝贵的领域知识，但其半结构化格式、隐式步骤属性和复杂的章节依赖关系使其难以直接用于测试自动化。为解决这一问题，我们生成了知识图谱（KG），以结构化形式捕获ESCM中的配置知识。我们提出了一种基于多智能体LLM的框架，通过细粒度的KG模式和迭代的提取-评估-改进（EEI）循环，从ESCM中提取、评估和改进KG。我们在50个真实ESCM上的评估表明，使用原始提示，我们的框架在所有三个提取任务中实现了高提取正确性，平均正确性得分在0.97到0.99之间。对于具有挑战性的ESCM，EEI循环通过专门的手动提示改进进一步提高了正确性。此外，LLM判断与人工评估显示出高度一致性，所有提取任务的Cohen's kappa至少为0.72。最后，来自行业测试人员的反馈表明，生成的KG可以支持为下游测试生成有用且正确的测试用例规范（TCS）。

Original abstract: Technical documents contain rich domain knowledge for automating downstream tasks such as system testing. While this paper focuses on Ethernet switch configuration manuals (ESCMs), we propose a general framework that can be adapted to different industrial contexts. ESCMs provide valuable domain knowledge for Ethernet switch testing, but their semi-structured format, implicit step attributes, and complex section dependencies make them difficult to directly leverage for test automation. To address this, we generate knowledge graphs (KGs) that capture configuration knowledge from ESCM in a structured form. We propose a multi-agent LLM-based framework that extracts, evaluates, and improves KGs from ESCMs using a fine-grained KG schema and an iterative Extract-Evaluate-Improve (EEI) loop. Our evaluation on 50 real-world ESCMs shows that our framework achieves high extraction correctness using the original prompts, with average correctness scores ranging from 0.97 to 0.99 across three extraction tasks. For challenging ESCMs, the EEI loop further improves correctness through manual-specific prompt refinement. Moreover, the LLM judgments and human evaluations show substantial agreement, with Cohen's kappa of at least 0.72 across all extraction tasks. Finally, feedback from industry testers indicates that the generated KGs can support the generation of useful and correct test case specifications (TCSs) for downstream testing.

</details>

### [16] [EXG: Self-Evolving Agents with Experience Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17721v1)
*Yuxin Jin,Siyuan Zhang,Hanchen Wang,Lu Qin,Ying Zhang,Wenjie Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出经验图框架实现自演进agent，在代码生成等任务上提升，直接相关

TL;DR: EXG是一种经验图框架，通过结构化积累成功和失败经验，显著提升了自进化智能体在代码生成和推理任务上的性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自进化智能体依赖临时反思或非结构化记忆，无法有效积累和复用跨任务经验，导致性能提升有限且资源效率低。

Method: 提出EXG经验图框架，将成功和失败经验组织成结构化关系图，支持在线实时增长和离线复用，可作为即插即用组件整合到现有自进化智能体中。

Result: 在代码生成和推理基准上，EXG在在线和离线评估中均优于基于反思和记忆的基线，实现了更好的性能-效率权衡。

Conclusion: 将经验结构化为图为可扩展和可迁移的自进化智能体行为提供了原则性基础。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的智能体通过多步交互在复杂推理和问题解决中展现出强大的能力，然而大多数已部署的智能体在行为上仍然是静态的，执行过程中获取的知识很少能随时间转化为系统性的改进。为此，关于自进化智能体的研究日益增多，探索智能体如何在部署过程中通过经验进行改进，但现有方法大多依赖于仅限于单任务纠正的临时反思，或采用非结构化记忆来积累碎片化经验，导致可用性延迟。为解决这一限制，我们引入了EXG，一种用于自进化智能体的经验图框架，它将积累的成功和失败显式组织成结构化的关系表示。EXG是首个专为自进化智能体设计的经验图，支持在执行过程中实时的在线图增长，以实现即时的跨任务经验复用，以及将整合后的经验图作为外部记忆模块进行离线复用。该设计还使EXG能够作为现有自进化智能体的即插即用组件，将先前经验组织成统一的经验图，随着部署的推进提高解决方案质量和资源效率。在代码生成和推理基准上的广泛实验表明，EXG在在线和离线评估中均比基于反思和记忆的基线获得了更优的性能-效率权衡。我们的结果表明，将经验构造成图结构为可扩展和可迁移的自进化智能体行为提供了原则性基础。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in complex reasoning and problem solving through multi-step interactions, yet most deployed agents remain behaviorally static, with knowledge acquired during execution rarely translating into systematic improvement over time. In response, a growing line of work on self-evolving agents explores how agents can improve through experience during deployment, but most existing approaches either rely on ad hoc reflection limited to single-task correction or adopt unstructured memory that accumulates fragmented experience with delayed usability. To address this limitation, we introduce EXG, an experience graph framework for self-evolving agents that explicitly organizes accumulated successes and failures into a structured, relational representation. EXG is the first experience graph designed for self-evolving agents, supporting both online, real-time graph growth during execution for immediate cross-task experience reuse, and offline reuse of a consolidated experience graph as an external memory module. This design also enables EXG to serve as a plug-and-play component for existing self-evolving agents, organizing prior experience into a unified experience graph and improving both solution quality and resource efficiency as deployment progresses. Extensive experiments across code generation and reasoning benchmarks show that EXG attains more favorable performance-efficiency trade-offs than reflection- and memory-based baselines in both online and offline evaluations. Our results suggest that structuring experience as a graph provides a principled foundation for scalable and transferable self-evolving agent behavior.

</details>


### [17] [Harnessing LLM Agents with Skill Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17734v1)
*Hongjun Liu,Yifei Ming,Shafiq Joty,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将技能编码为可执行程序函数，干预agent循环，提升复杂任务性能，直接相关

TL;DR: HASP将技能升级为可执行程序函数（PFs），作为可执行的防护栏在推理或训练后干预LLM智能体循环，显著提升网页搜索、数学推理和编码任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于文本的经验指导缺乏明确的干预机制，无法在智能体循环中主动介入，限制了复杂长时任务的执行效果。

Method: 提出HASP框架，将技能转化为可执行程序函数（PFs），并在推理时、训练后或自我进化阶段模块化应用，以修改动作或注入纠正上下文。

Result: 在网页搜索推理中，推理时PFs使平均性能相比ReAct提升25%，训练后与受控进化相比Search-R1提升30.4%。

Conclusion: HASP通过可执行程序函数有效提升了LLM智能体性能，机制分析揭示了PFs的触发与干预机制、技能内化过程及稳定技能库进化的要求。

中文摘要：赋予LLM智能体从过去经验中衍生的可复用技能已成为处理复杂且长期任务的一种流行且成功的方法。然而，这些经验教训通常被编码为文本指导，在很大程度上仅起到建议作用，缺乏明确机制来规定何时以及如何干预智能体循环。为弥合这一差距，我们引入了HASP（Harnessing LLM Agents with Skill Programs），这是一个新框架，将技能升级为可执行程序函数（PFs）。PFs不是提供被动建议，而是作为可执行的防护栏，在容易失败的状态下激活，修改下一步行动或注入纠正性上下文。HASP高度模块化：它可以在推理时应用以直接干预智能体循环，在训练后提供结构化监督，或通过进化经过验证且由教师审查的PF实现自我改进。实证结果表明，与无训练和基于训练的方法相比，HASP在网页搜索、数学推理和编码任务上均取得了显著收益。例如，在网页搜索推理中，仅推理时的PF就将平均性能相比（多循环）ReAct智能体提升了25%，而训练后与受控进化相比Search-R1实现了30.4%的提升。为深入理解HASP，我们的机制分析揭示了PFs如何触发和干预、技能如何内化以及稳定技能库进化的要求。

Original abstract: Equipping LLM agents with reusable skills derived from past experience has become a popular and successful approach for tackling complex and long-horizon tasks. However, such lessons are often encoded as textual guidance that remains largely advisory, lacking explicit mechanisms for when and how to intervene in the agent loop. To bridge the gap, we introduce HASP(Harnessing LLM Agents with Skill Programs), a new framework that upgrades skills into executable Program Functions (PFs). Rather than offering passive advice, PFs act as executable guardrails that activate on failure-prone states and modify the next action or inject corrective context. HASP is highly modular: it can be applied at inference time for direct agent-loop intervention, during post-training to provide structured supervision, or for self-improvement by evolving validated, teacher-reviewed PFs. Empirically, HASP drives substantial gains compared to both training-free and training-based methods on web-search, math reasoning, and coding tasks. For example, on web-search reasoning, inference-time PFs alone improve the average performance by 25% compared to (multi-loop) ReAct Agent, while post-training and controlled evolution achieve a 30.4% gain over Search-R1. To provide deeper insights into HASP, our mechanism analysis reveals how PFs trigger and intervene, how skills are internalized, and the requirement for stable skill library evolution.

### [18] [Agents for Experiments, Experiments for Agents: A Design Grammar for AI-Enabled Experimental Science](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17746v1)
*Yingjie Zhang,Chun Feng,Weizhang Zhu,Tianshu Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出SEED框架描述agent实验条件，对agent workflow设计有潜在启发

TL;DR: 提出SEED框架，用结构化图表示AI实验条件，支持描述、评估和生成，初步测试显示其作为设计辅助的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统实验条件用散文描述，难以比较、重用或审计，需要更好的表示方法以支持人机交互和智能体工作流的研究。

Method: 引入SEED框架，将实验条件表示为类型化的参与者-流程图，支持描述交互结构、评估结构新颖性和在约束下生成候选设计。

Result: 在医疗分诊任务中，SEED引导的候选设计比无图指导更清晰地展示参与者-流程变化、假设和治理检查，验证了框架的可行性。

Conclusion: SEED有助于解决工作流表示和治理问题，但需注意新颖性、可复制性、有效性、探究多样性和问责制等治理张力。

中文摘要：人工智能系统正成为组织和知识工作中的积极参与者。它们越来越多地与人类互动、协调工作流程，并在多智能体安排中运作。因此，理解它们的影响不仅需要衡量输出准确性，还需要关于机制、委托、反馈和控制的证据。实验仍然是这一任务的核心，但它们也面临一个递归挑战：我们需要实验来研究这些安排中的智能体，并且我们可能需要智能体来帮助实验以探索不断扩大的设计空间。然而，人机交互和智能体工作流的实验条件仍然大多以散文形式指定，这使得它们难以比较、重用或审计。我们将此视为人工智能赋能知识生产中的工作流表示、可追溯性和治理问题。我们引入了SEED（实验发现的结构化编码），这是一个将实验条件表示为类型化的参与者-流程图的框架。SEED支持三种设计功能：将条件描述为交互结构，评估相对于编码的先前设计的结构新颖性，以及在可行性和治理约束下生成候选设计。我们报告了一个轻量级的实证可行性测试，该测试在医疗分诊设计任务中比较了无图指导和SEED引导的生成。在这种诊断对比中，SEED引导的候选设计显示出更清晰的参与者-流程变化、假设和治理检查，支持了该语法作为设计辅助工具的可行性。评论最后指出了关于新颖性、可复制性、有效性、探究多样性和问责制的治理张力。

Original abstract: AI systems are becoming active participants in organizational and knowledge work. They increasingly interact with humans, coordinate workflows, and operate in multi-agent arrangements. Understanding their effects therefore requires more than measuring output accuracy; it requires evidence about mechanisms, delegation, feedback, and control. Experiments remain central to this task, but they also face a recursive challenge: we need experiments for agents to study these arrangements, and we may need agents for experiments to help search the expanding space of possible designs. Yet experimental conditions for human-AI and agentic workflows are still largely specified in prose, making them difficult to compare, reuse, or audit. We frame this as a problem of workflow representation, traceability, and governance in AI-enabled knowledge production. We introduce SEED (Structural Encoding for Experimental Discovery), a framework that represents experimental conditions as typed actor-flow graphs. SEED supports three design functions: describing conditions as interaction structures, evaluating structural novelty relative to encoded prior designs, and generating candidate designs under feasibility and governance constraints. We report a lightweight empirical feasibility test that compares graph-blind and SEEDguided generation in a medical-triage design task. In this diagnostic contrast, SEED-guided candidate designs show clearer actor-flow changes, assumptions, and governance checks, supporting the feasibility of the grammar as a design aid. The commentary closes by identifying governance tensions around novelty, replication, validity, diversity of inquiry, and accountability.

### [19] [STRIDE: A Self-Reflective Agent Framework for Reliable Automatic Equation Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17790v1)
*Jiarui Su,Songjun Tu,Bei Sun,Xiaojun Liang*

Selection reason: 自反思agent框架用于自动方程发现，可迁移至代码优化agent的自我改进

TL;DR: STRIDE是一个自我反思的智能体框架，通过协调数据感知生成、混合拟合评估、批评者-执行者修复和多样性语义记忆，提高了基于LLM的符号方程发现的可靠性和性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出STRIDE框架，包含数据感知生成、混合拟合评估、批评者-执行者修复和多样性保持的语义记忆，通过共享反馈实现闭环发现。

Result: 在符号回归基准和LSR-Synth套件上，STRIDE在多个LLM骨干上提高了准确性、OOD鲁棒性和结构恢复，消融实验证实了核心组件的贡献。

Original abstract: LLM-based equation discovery offers a promising route to recovering symbolic laws from data, but many systems still rely on generation-centered loops that propose candidates, fit parameters, score results, and reuse selected examples. Such loops can misjudge useful skeletons under unreliable fitting, discard near-correct equations that require repair, and accumulate redundant memories that provide limited guidance. We propose STRIDE, a self-reflective agent framework that improves reliability by coordinating data-aware generation, mixed-fitting evaluation, critic--executor repair, and diversity-preserving semantic memory. By turning fitted scores and candidate behavior into shared feedback, STRIDE enables equations to be proposed, assessed, refined, and reused within a closed-loop discovery process. Experiments on representative symbolic-regression benchmarks and LSR-Synth suites show that STRIDE improves accuracy, OOD robustness, and structural recovery across multiple LLM backbones, with ablations and analyses confirming the contribution of its core components.

### [20] [Interactive Evaluation Requires a Design Science](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17829v1)
*Keyang Xuan,Peiyang Song,Pan Lu,Pengrui Han,Wenkai Li,Zhenyu Zhang,Zexue He,Wenyue Hua,Manling Li,Jiaxuan You,Adrian Weller,Yizhong Wang,Jiaxin Pei*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI评估从静态基准转向交互式系统，但缺乏统一的评估范式，导致评估混乱。

Method: 通过定义评估为从证据到判断的映射，分析交互式评估带来的变化，提出两轴分类法、设计原则和报告标准。

Result: 提出了一个包含两轴分类法、设计原则和报告标准的交互式评估框架，并分析了轨迹层面的挑战。

Conclusion: 交互式评估需要全新的范式，简单沿用旧范式无法适用，本文框架为未来评估提供了指导。

中文摘要：AI评估正在经历结构性变化。大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被部署为通过工具、环境、用户和其他智能体随时间行动的系统，而许多评估实践仍然继承自基于响应的基准（例如，固定输入、孤立输出以及可从单个响应中做出的结果判断）。该领域已开始构建交互式基准，但由此产生的格局是碎片化的：基准在允许哪些交互产物、如何对轨迹进行评分以及其结果支持哪些主张方面存在差异。本文立场论文认为，交互式评估应被视为一种原则性的评估范式，而不仅仅是一类新的智能体基准。简单地采用先前的评估范式是不够的。我们将评估定义为从证据到判断的自主映射，并表明交互式评估改变了这一映射的两方面：证据变为交互生成的轨迹，而评估过程必须评估过程、可恢复性、协调性、鲁棒性和系统级性能。基于这一定义，我们提出了一个两轴分类法，推导出设计原则和报告标准，考察了代表性场景，并分析了长期存在的评估挑战如何在轨迹层面重新出现。

Original abstract: AI evaluation is undergoing a structural change. Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as systems that act over time through tools, environments, users, and other agents, while many evaluation practices still inherit assumptions from response-centered benchmarks (e.g., fixed inputs, isolated outputs, and outcome judgments that can be made from a single response). The field has begun to build interactive benchmarks, but the resulting landscape is fragmented: benchmarks differ in what interaction artifacts they admit, how trajectories are scored, and what claims their results support. This position paper argues that interactive evaluation should be treated as a principled evaluation paradigm, not merely a new family of agent benchmarks. Simply adopting previous evaluation paradigms does not suffice. We define evaluation as an autonomous mapping from evidence to judgments, and show that interactive evaluation changes both sides of this mapping: the evidence becomes interaction-generated trajectories, while the evaluation procedure must assess process, recoverability, coordination, robustness, and system-level performance. Building on this definition, we propose a two-axis taxonomy, derive design principles and reporting standards, examine representative scenarios, and analyze how longstanding evaluation challenges reappear at the trajectory level.

### [21] [Remembering More, Risking More: Longitudinal Safety Risks in Memory-Equipped LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17830v1)
*Ahmad Al-Tawaha,Shangding Gu,Peizhi Niu,Ruoxi Jia,Ming Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究记忆LLM agent的长期安全性，与agent记忆和安全相关。

TL;DR: 研究了配备记忆的LLM智能体在长时间跨独立任务中因记忆积累导致的安全风险（时间记忆污染），通过触发-探测协议和NullMemory基线发现了随记忆长度增加的违规趋势，并验证了记忆内容而非顺序是主要因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全评估仅关注单任务内的安全，忽略了智能体在长期服务中记忆跨任务积累带来的安全风险，因此需要评估时间维度上的安全变化。

Method: 提出触发-探测协议，在不同前缀长度的记忆快照上评估固定探测集，并使用NullMemory反事实基线识别记忆引起的违规；在多个场景和记忆架构上实验，并进行了顺序随机化实验。

Result: 记忆智能体违规率持续超过无记忆基线，且随记忆长度增加而上升；顺序随机化表明内容积累而非顺序是关键；风险可在生成前从检索状态检测到。

Conclusion: 记忆安全应视为纵向属性，需要时间评估，而非单一快照评估。

中文摘要：对配备记忆的LLM智能体进行安全评估通常衡量任务内安全性：即智能体是否在单个场景中安全完成任务，通常是在对抗条件下，例如提示注入或记忆中毒。然而，在部署中，单个智能体在长时间跨度内服务于许多独立任务，并且在早期任务中积累的记忆可能会影响后续不相关任务的行为。研究这一机制需要跨任务的时间维度评估：不仅评估智能体在单一记忆状态下是否安全，还要评估随着跨多个独立交互的记忆积累，其安全状况如何变化。我们将这种失败模式称为时间记忆污染。为了将记忆暴露与流非平稳性分离，我们引入了一种触发-探测协议，该协议针对不同前缀长度的只读记忆快照评估固定的探测集，同时结合NullMemory反事实基线来识别由记忆引起的违规。我们将此协议应用于三个部署场景（涵盖记录、备忘录、表格和电子邮件通信）和八种记忆架构，并额外应用于类似Claw的AI智能体（如OpenClaw），使用该平台的原生记忆机制。配备记忆的智能体始终超过NullMemory基线，并且由记忆引起的违规率在两类智能体上均显示出随暴露长度增长的强劲上升趋势。顺序随机化实验表明，这种效应主要由积累的内容驱动，而非遭遇顺序。最后，事件分解的一个结构性结果是，记忆引起的风险可以在生成之前从检索状态中检测到，我们通过一个高召回率的诊断监控器证实了这一点。我们的结果主张将记忆安全性视为一种纵向属性，需要时间评估，而非一种可以通过快照捕获的单一状态属性。

Original abstract: Safety evaluations of memory-equipped LLM agents typically measure within-task safety: whether an agent completes a single scenario safely, often under adversarial conditions such as prompt injection or memory poisoning. In deployment, however, a single agent serves many independent tasks over a long horizon, and memory accumulated during earlier tasks can affect behavior on later, unrelated ones. Studying this regime requires evaluation along the temporal dimension across tasks: not whether an agent is safe at any single memory state, but how its safety profile changes as memory accumulates across many independent interactions. We call this failure mode temporal memory contamination. To isolate memory exposure from stream non-stationarity, we introduce a trigger-probe protocol that evaluates a fixed probe set against read-only memory snapshots at varying prefix lengths, together with a NullMemory counterfactual baseline for identifying memory-induced violations. We apply this protocol across three deployment scenarios spanning records, memos, forms, and email correspondence and eight memory architectures, and additionally on Claw-like AI agents, such as OpenClaw, using the platform's native memory mechanism. Memory-enabled agents consistently exceed the NullMemory baseline, and memory-induced violation rates show a robust upward trend with exposure length on both agent classes. Order-randomization experiments indicate that the effect is driven primarily by accumulated content rather than encounter order. Finally, a structural consequence of the event decomposition is that memory-induced risk is detectable from retrieval state before generation, which we confirm with a high-recall diagnostic monitor. Our results argue for treating memory safety as a longitudinal property that requires temporal evaluation, not a single-state property that can be captured by a snapshot.

</details>


### [22] [KISS - Knowledge Infrastructure for Scientific Simulation: A Scaffolding for Agentic Earth Science](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17856v1)
*Ziwei Li,Liujun Zhu,Yuchen Liu,Yichen Zhao,Birk Li,Ruiqi Wu,Junliang Jin,Jianyun Zhang*

TL;DR: 提出知识基础设施（KI），使非专业代理能够端到端执行基于过程的仿真模型，显著提升模拟成功率并降低访问与整合障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最易受气候风险和资源匮乏影响的社区无法使用基于过程的仿真模型，需要降低其使用门槛。

Method: 构建知识基础设施（KI），包含验证的建模算子、分阶段领域协议和诊断恢复机制；并开发知识剖析工具包（KDT）自动生成KI。

Result: 在3000次试验中，配备KI的代理成功率达84%，无KI的代理低于40%；KDT能生成119个跨14个地球科学领域的KI，且建模决策和故障修复趋同。

Conclusion: KI降低了非专业用户与过程模拟之间的访问障碍以及建模社区间的整合障碍，使过程科学成为活的科学公共资源。

中文摘要：基于过程的仿真模型编码了地球科学几十年的科学理解，然而最暴露于气候风险和资源匮乏的社区最无法使用它们。在这里，我们引入知识基础设施（KI），一种代理可操作的框架，将专业知识外化为经过验证的建模算子、分阶段领域协议和诊断恢复机制。在3000次试验的耦合水文基准测试中，配备KI的代理在高达84%的试验中产生了物理上合理、可验证的端到端模拟，而没有KI的代理停滞在40%以下。KI跨学科通用。我们将构建过程打包成知识剖析工具包（KDT），它自主生成KI，使得端到端代理执行跨越14个地球科学领域的117个额外基于过程的模型成为可能。在所有119个KI中，尽管底层物理不同，建模决策和故障修复趋同，表明操作专业知识是结构化和可提取的，而非临时的。演示表明配备KI的代理降低了非专业用户与基于过程模拟之间的访问障碍，以及建模社区之间的整合障碍。通过这种框架，基于过程的科学可以演变为一个活的科学公共资源，对需要知道的人负责，并由能够贡献的人扩展。

Original abstract: Process-based simulation models encode decades of scientific understanding across the Earth sciences, yet the communities most exposed to climate risk and resource scarcity are the least able to use them. Here, we introduce knowledge infrastructure (KI), an agent-actionable scaffold that externalizes expertise into validated modelling operators, staged domain protocols, and diagnostic recovery mechanisms. Across a 3,000-trial coupled-hydrology benchmark, agents equipped with KI produced physically plausible, verifiable end-to-end simulations in up to 84% of trials, while agents without KI plateaued below 40%. KI generalizes across disciplines. We packaged its construction into a Knowledge Dissection Toolkit (KDT) that autonomously produced KI enabling end-to-end agent execution of 117 additional process-based models across 14 Earth-science domains. Across all 119 KIs, modelling decisions and failure remedies converged despite different underlying physics, showing that operational expertise is structured and extractable rather than ad hoc. Demonstrations show KI-equipped agents lowering both the access barrier between non-specialist users and process-based simulation, and the integration barrier between modelling communities. Through this scaffold, process-based science can then evolve as a living scientific commons, answerable to whoever needs to know and extendable by whoever can contribute.

</details>


### [23] [PAIR: Prefix-Aware Internal Reward Model for Multi-Turn Agent Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17877v1)
*Wonjoong Kim,Yeonjun In,Sangwu Park,Dongha Lee,Chanyoung Park*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出前缀感知内部奖励模型，解决多轮agent优化中的信用分配问题，可直接迁移至coding agent的奖励设计与训练

TL;DR: 提出PAIR方法，利用隐藏状态探针和注意力头的组合提供步骤级奖励，解决GRPO在复杂任务中的信用分配问题，成本低且无需外部依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO依赖稀疏结果奖励，导致多步任务中的信用分配困难；现有解决方案成本高或受限于实际条件，亟需一种低成本、无外部依赖的步骤级奖励信号。

Method: 提出PAIR（前缀感知内部奖励），一个两阶段模型：冻结的隐藏状态探针估计信念一致性，轻量级注意力头将其纠正为基于真实正确性，两者互补以实现对污染和干净轨迹的鲁棒性。

Result: 在污染轨迹上，PAIR实现了最高的AUROC，且推理成本可忽略不计；无需外部模型调用、真实答案依赖或完整轨迹展开即可提供密集步骤级奖励。

Conclusion: PAIR能为GRPO训练提供有效的步骤级奖励信号，克服了现有方法的局限，具有低成本和高鲁棒性的优势。

中文摘要：当前LLMs面临的一个重大障碍是执行复杂的多阶段任务。组相对策略优化（GRPO）已成为一种领先选择，但其对稀疏结果奖励的依赖严重限制了跨中间步骤的信用分配。现有的补救措施，例如运行完整轨迹以分配步骤级优势、在每一步调用外部LLM法官、或计算需要在每次评估时提供真实答案的内在奖励，都会带来显著的成本或实际限制。我们假设，LLM隐藏状态上的内部正确性探测可以被重新用作步骤级奖励信号，可能一次性解决所有这些限制。然而，现有的探测研究假设输入是干净的，我们首先表明这一假设在多步设置中失效：隐藏状态探测在前缀污染下严重退化——跟踪与（可能被污染的）前缀的连贯性而非基于真实正确性，而基于注意力的特征对污染保持鲁棒，但在干净前缀上表现不佳。基于这种互补关系，我们提出了前缀感知内部奖励（PAIR），这是一个两阶段模型，包含一个冻结的隐藏状态探针用于估计信念一致性，以及一个轻量级的注意力头用于将其纠正为基于真实正确性。实验结果表明，PAIR在污染轨迹上实现了最高的AUROC，同时推理成本可忽略不计，为GRPO训练提供了密集的步骤级奖励信号，无需外部模型调用、真实答案依赖或完整轨迹展开。

Original abstract: A significant hurdle for current LLMs is the execution of complex, multi-stage tasks. Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has been emerging as a leading choice, but its reliance on sparse outcome rewards severely limits credit assignment across intermediate steps. Existing remedies such as running full rollouts to assign step-level advantages, calling external LLM judges at each step, or computing intrinsic rewards that require ground-truth answers at every evaluation introduce significant costs or practical constraints. We hypothesize that internal correctness probing over LLM hidden states can be repurposed as a step-level reward signal, potentially addressing all of these limitations at once. However, existing probing research assumes clean inputs, and we first show that this assumption breaks down in multi-step settings: hidden-state probes degrade severely under prefix contamination tracking coherence with the (possibly corrupted) prefix rather than grounded correctness, while attention-based features remain robust to contamination but underperform on clean prefixes. Building on this complementary relationship, we propose the Prefix-Aware Internal Reward (PAIR), a two-stage model with a frozen hidden-state probe estimating belief-consistency and a lightweight attention-based head correcting it toward grounded correctness. Experimental results show that PAIR achieves the highest AUROC on contaminated trajectories while operating at negligible inference cost, enabling dense step-level reward signals for GRPO training without external model calls, ground-truth dependencies, or full-trajectory rollouts.

Original abstract: While agentic AI and its core multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have demonstrated remarkable promise in language and visual reasoning across domains ranging from daily life to advanced scientific research, a profound gap remains between artificial and human intelligence. Despite the integration of powerful tools and advanced MLLMs, state-of-the-art AI agents frequently fail at foundational, seemingly simple tasks that a child can resolve with ease. Inspired by the Wechsler Intelligence Scale for Children (WISC), we introduce ChildAgentEval, the first psychometrically grounded interactive benchmark for evaluating cognitive age alignment in MLLM-based agents. ### [25] [LAST-RAG: Literature-Anchored Stochastic Trajectory Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Knowledge-Conditioned Degradation Model Selection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17902v1)
*Hanbyeol Park,Hyerim Bae*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出知识条件RAG用于退化模型选择，虽领域非软件工程，但RAG是agent通用组件，有一定可迁移性

TL;DR: 本文提出LAST-RAG方法，利用观测数据和领域知识进行退化模型选择，优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型选择方法仅依赖观测HI轨迹的统计拟合，在短窗口或高噪声下可能选出与退化机制不一致的模型。

Method: 提出LAST-RAG，结合观测HI轨迹和领域上下文，从本地证据库检索证据以分层约束候选模型空间；并引入RCRUS防止不确定时过早淘汰候选模型。

Result: 仿真实验表明，LAST-RAG在Wiener/gamma族分类和详细模型分类上均优于统计、预测和不确定性感知基线。

Conclusion: 将退化模型选择从统计拟合问题重新定义为知识条件决策问题，整合观测数据与领域知识。

中文摘要：基于随机过程的退化建模是估计剩余使用寿命（RUL）分布的核心方法；然而，合适的随机过程选择问题尚未得到充分解决。现有的模型选择方法主要依赖于观测健康指标（HI）轨迹的统计拟合，但当观测窗口较短或信号高度噪声时，这种方法可能选择与潜在退化机制不一致的模型。为解决这一问题，本文提出了文献锚定的随机轨迹检索增强生成（LAST-RAG）。该方法同时利用观测的HI轨迹和领域特定上下文，基于从本地证据库中检索到的理论和机械证据，分层地条件化候选退化模型空间。此外，引入了基于规则的不确定状态置信推理（RCRUS），以防止在分层决策不确定时候选模型被过早淘汰。基于仿真的实验表明，所提出的方法在Wiener/gamma族分类以及详细退化模型分类方面均优于统计、预测和不确定性感知基线。最终，本研究将退化模型选择从纯粹的统计拟合优度问题重新定义为一种知识条件决策问题，该问题整合了观测数据与领域知识。

Original abstract: Stochastic-process-based degradation modeling is a core approach for estimating the distribution of remaining useful life (RUL); however, the selection of an appropriate stochastic process has not been sufficiently addressed. Existing model selection methods mainly rely on the statistical fit of the observed health indicator (HI) trajectory, but this approach may select a model that is inconsistent with the underlying degradation mechanism when the observation window is short or the signal is highly noisy. To address this issue, this paper proposes Literature-Anchored Stochastic Trajectory Retrieval-Augmented Generation (LAST-RAG). The proposed method uses both the observed HI trajectory and domain-specific context, and hierarchically conditions the candidate degradation model space based on theoretical and mechanical evidence retrieved from a local evidence bank. In addition, Rule-based Confidence Reasoning with Uncertain State (RCRUS) is introduced to prevent candidate models from being prematurely eliminated when hierarchical decisions are uncertain. Simulation-based experiments demonstrate that the proposed method outperforms statistical, prognostic, and uncertainty-aware baselines in both Wiener/gamma family classification and detailed degradation model classification. Ultimately, this study reframes degradation model selection from a purely statistical goodness-of-fit problem into a knowledge-conditioned decision-making problem that integrates observed data with domain knowledge.

### [26] [Agentic Chunking and Bayesian De-chunking of AI Generated Fuzzy Cognitive Maps: A Model of the Thucydides Trap](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17903v1)
*Akash Kumar Panda,Olaoluwa Adigun,Bart Kosko*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用LLM agent进行文本分块和因果图生成，agentic chunking方法可迁移至代码agent中的上下文分割

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用大语言模型将文本分块并混合成因果模糊认知图（FCM）的方法，通过凸混合和稀疏矩阵运算实现可扩展的因果推理，并在修昔底德陷阱文本上验证，多数FCM预测战争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动从文本生成因果知识图谱，利用LLM的文本理解能力实现高效的分块和混合，以支持结构化的因果推理和贝叶斯更新。

Method: 使用LLM代理将文本分解为重叠的文本块，每个块生成FCM，通过凸混合得到循环FCM知识图谱，利用稀疏因果块矩阵实现轻量计算，并支持操作符级别的贝叶斯推理产生去块化后验FCM。

Result: 在修昔底德陷阱模型文本上，8个FCM知识图谱中有7个在刺激崛起力量野心和权利概念节点时预测了战争类型。

Conclusion: 该混合技术有效且可扩展，能够从文本中自动生成因果FCM，并产生有用的去块化后验FCM，支持进一步贝叶斯更新迭代。

中文摘要：我们通过教授大语言模型代理将文本分解为重叠的文本块，自动从文本生成反馈因果模糊认知图（FCM）。这些块FCM的凸混合产生一个代表性的循环FCM知识图谱。文本块可以有不同的重叠程度。块FCM仍然混合形成一个新的FCM因果知识图谱。混合技术可扩展，因为它使用稀疏因果块矩阵进行轻量计算。混合结构允许操作符级别的贝叶斯推理，从混合FCM中产生“去块化”或后验式的FCM。这些去块化FCM本身有用，并允许进一步的贝叶斯更新迭代。我们在Allison的“修昔底德陷阱”模型的文章文本上展示了这些混合技术，该模型描述了如美国这样的主导力量与如中国这样的崛起力量之间的冲突。FCM动态系统在平衡到不动点或极限环吸引子时预测结果。当我们通过打开并保持代表崛起力量野心和权利的概念节点来刺激它们时，8个FCM知识图谱中有7个预测了一种战争类型。Gemini 3.1 LLMs作为分块AI代理。

Original abstract: We automatically generate feedback causal fuzzy cognitive maps (FCMs) from text by teaching large-language-model agents to break the text into overlapping chunks of text. Convex mixing of these chunk FCMs gives a representative cyclic FCM knowledge graph. The text chunks can have different levels of overlap. The chunk FCMs still mix to form a new FCM causal knowledge graph. The mixing technique scales because it uses light computation with sparse causal chunk matrices. The mixing structure allows an operator-level type of Bayesian inference that produces "de-chunked" or posterior-like FCMs from the mixed FCM. These de-chunked FCMs are useful in their own right and allow further iterations of Bayesian updating. We demonstrate these mixing techniques on the essay text of Allison's "Thucydides Trap" model of conflict between a dominant power such as the United States and a rising power such as China. The FCM dynamical systems predict outcomes as they equilibrate to fixed-point or limit-cycle attractors. Seven out of 8 FCM knowledge graphs predicted a type of war when we stimulated them by turning on and keeping on the concept node that stands for the rising power's ambition and entitlement. Gemini 3.1 LLMs served as the chunking AI agents.

</details>


### [27] [Ethical Hyper-Velocity (EHV): A Hardware-Rooted Zero-Trust Runtime Enforcement Architecture for Agentic AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17909v2)
*Riddhi Mohan Sharma*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 面向agent系统的硬件根信任运行时强制架构，涉及安全控制和策略执行，可迁移至coding agent的安全保障设计

TL;DR: EHV是一种集成GCD、因果CRDT、TEE证明和形式验证的硬件根源强制执行架构，将治理延迟从天数降低到常数时间，并通过TLA+验证零违规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有回溯审计框架（如ISO/IEC 42001）存在14-30天的策略延迟，无法满足高频策略更新的安全需求。

Method: 结合语法约束解码（GCD）、因果图CRDT策略同步、TEE证明执行、OSCAL审计日志以及治理感知JIT编译器，并将策略执行点嵌入推理流水线。

Result: TLA+模型检查证明在1,738个状态（324个不同状态，深度8）中零违规，实现O(1)运行时强制执行，治理延迟从O(天数)降至O(1)。

Conclusion: EHV通过硬件根源的集成架构有效消除部署速度与治理完整性之间的权衡，适用于儿科肿瘤剂量等关键基础设施场景。

中文摘要：随着自主代理系统在受监管的关键基础设施中扩展，缺乏机械化的、硬件根源的高频策略更新执行机制构成了基本的安全缺口。我们提出了伦理超速（EHV），一种用于代理系统的治理感知运行时强制执行架构，它结合了语法约束解码（GCD）用于内联策略约束的令牌生成、基于因果图CRDT的向量时钟排序策略同步、可信执行环境（TEE）中的硬件证明执行以及OSCAL格式的机器可读审计日志。与引入14-30天策略延迟的回溯审计框架（ISO/IEC 42001、NIST AI RMF）不同，EHV通过治理感知即时（JIT）编译器将策略执行点（PEP）重新定位到推理流水线中。在明确陈述的假设下，该架构减少了强制执行延迟，提高了可追溯性，并支持在有界模型中对安全不变量的形式验证。我们通过TLA+模型检查证明，在验证的有界操作状态空间（生成1,738个状态，324个不同状态，深度8，零违规）中，不合规的代理动作是不可达的。在这些条件下，O(1)运行时强制执行减少了部署速度与治理完整性之间的传统权衡，将治理延迟从O(天数)降低到O(1)。EHV的区别性贡献是将GCD、因果CRDT、TEE证明缓存和有界形式验证集成到一个单一的、硬件根源的强制执行架构中——这是任何同期系统都未实现的组合。该架构通过儿科肿瘤剂量用例进行演示，并适用于包括医疗、金融合规和关键基础设施控制在内的受监管关键基础设施。

Original abstract: As autonomous agentic systems scale across regulated critical infrastructures, the lack of mechanistic, hardware-rooted enforcement for high-frequency policy updates presents a fundamental safety gap. We present Ethical Hyper-Velocity (EHV), a governance-aware runtime enforcement architecture for agentic systems that combines Grammar-Constrained Decoding (GCD) for inline policy-constrained token generation, Causal Graph CRDT-based policy synchronization with vector-clock ordering, hardware-attested execution in Trusted Execution Environments (TEEs), and OSCAL-formatted machine-readable audit logging. Unlike retrospective auditing frameworks (ISO/IEC 42001, NIST AI RMF) that introduce 14-30 day policy latencies, EHV relocates the Policy Enforcement Point (PEP) into the inference pipeline via a Governance-Aware Just-In-Time (JIT) Compiler. Under explicitly stated assumptions, the architecture reduces enforcement latency, improves traceability, and supports formal verification of safety invariants in a bounded model. We demonstrate via TLA+ model checking that non-compliant agentic actions were unreachable in the verified bounded operating state space (1,738 states generated, 324 distinct, depth 8, zero violations). Under these conditions, O(1) runtime enforcement reduces the traditional trade-off between deployment velocity and governance integrity, targeting Governance Latency from O(days) toward O(1). EHV's differentiating contribution is the integration of GCD, Causal CRDT, TEE attestation caching, and bounded formal verification into a single, hardware-rooted enforcement architecture -- a combination not achieved by any contemporaneous system. The architecture is demonstrated through a pediatric oncology dosage use case, with applicability to regulated critical infrastructures including healthcare, financial compliance, and critical infrastructure control.

</details>


### [28] [Unleashing LLMs in Bayesian Optimization: Preference-Guided Framework for Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17976v1)
*Xinzhe Yuan,Zhuo Chen,Jianshu Zhang,Huan Xiong,Nanyang Ye,Yuqiang Li,Qinying Gu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM 偏好引导贝叶斯优化框架，可迁移至自动调参或代码优化中的超参数搜索。

TL;DR: 提出LGBO框架，将LLM偏好持续整合到贝叶斯优化循环中，通过区域提升偏好机制加速收敛，理论保证不显著差于标准BO，实验在多个科学领域基准和电池电解质优化中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学发现受限于昂贵实验和有限资源，需要高效优化；标准贝叶斯优化冷启动慢、高维可扩展性差，现有LLM辅助方法仅用于冷启动或候选生成，未持续整合LLM推理。

Method: 提出LLM-Guided Bayesian Optimization (LGBO)，引入区域提升偏好机制，将LLM驱动的偏好嵌入每次迭代，以稳定可控方式调整代理均值，保证worst-case表现不显著差于标准BO。

Result: 在物理、化学、生物学、材料科学干燥基准中一致优于现有方法；在铁铬电池电解质湿实验室优化中，6次迭代达到最佳观测值90%，而基线需10次以上。

Conclusion: LGBO为将LLM整合到科学优化流程提供了有前景的方向。

中文摘要：科学发现日益受到昂贵实验和有限资源的制约，凸显了在人工智能驱动的科学中高效优化的需求。贝叶斯优化（BO）虽因平衡探索与利用而被广泛采用，但在高维环境中常表现冷启动慢且可扩展性差，限制了其在现实科学问题中的适用性。为克服这些挑战，我们提出了LLM引导的贝叶斯优化（LGBO），这是首个将大语言模型（LLM）的语义推理持续整合到优化循环中的LLM偏好引导BO框架。与先前仅将LLM用于冷启动初始化或候选生成的工作不同，LGBO引入了一种区域提升偏好机制，将LLM驱动的偏好嵌入到每次迭代中，以稳定且可控的方式改变代理均值。理论上，我们证明了在 worst-case 情况下 LGBO 的表现不会显著差于标准 BO，而当偏好与目标一致时，收敛速度显著加快。实验上，LGBO 在物理、化学、生物学和材料科学等领域的多个干燥基准测试中一致优于现有方法。最值得注意的是，在一个新的铁铬电池电解液湿实验室优化中，LGBO 在6次迭代内达到了最佳观测值的90%，而标准 BO 和现有 LLM 增强基线需要超过10次。这些结果共同表明，LGBO 为将 LLM 整合到科学优化流程中提供了一个有前景的方向。

Original abstract: Scientific discovery is increasingly constrained by costly experiments and limited resources, underscoring the need for efficient optimization in AI for science. Bayesian Optimization (BO), though widely adopted for balancing exploration and exploitation, often exhibits slow cold-start performance and poor scalability in high-dimensional settings, limiting its applicability in real-world scientific problems. To overcome these challenges, we propose LLM-Guided Bayesian Optimization (LGBO), the first LLM preference-guided BO framework that continuously integrates the semantic reasoning of large language models (LLMs) into the optimization loop. Unlike prior works that use LLMs only for warm-start initialization or candidate generation, LGBO introduces a region-lifted preference mechanism that embeds LLM-driven preferences into every iteration, shifting the surrogate mean in a stable and controllable way. Theoretically, we prove that LGBO does not perform significantly worse than standard BO in the worst case, while achieving significantly faster convergence when preferences align with the objective. Empirically, LGBO consistently outperforms existing methods across diverse dry benchmarks in physics, chemistry, biology, and materials science. Most notably, in a new wet-lab optimization of Fe-Cr battery electrolytes, LGBO attains \textbf{90\% of the best observed value within 6 iterations}, whereas standard BO and existing LLM-augmented baselines require more than 10. Together, these results suggest that LGBO offers a promising direction for integrating LLMs into scientific optimization workflows.

</details>


### [29] [DocOS: Towards Proactive Document-Guided Actions in GUI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18048v1)
*Jingjing Liu,Ziye Huang,Zihao Cheng,Zeming Liu,Jiahong Wu,Yuhang Guo,Kehai Chen,Yunhong Wang,Haifeng Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI代理依赖静态参数知识，无法处理需要显式程序性知识的长尾任务，常陷入低效试错。

Method: 提出主动文档引导操作范式，使代理自主搜索文档；构建DocOS基准，在完全交互环境中评估文档引导的问题解决。

中文摘要：尽管图形用户界面（GUI）代理在自动化设备交互方面表现出了良好的性能，但它们主要依赖于预训练或指令调优中的静态参数知识。这种依赖从根本上限制了它们处理长尾任务的能力，这些任务需要模型参数中不存在的显式程序性知识，通常迫使代理诉诸低效且脆弱的试错探索。为了缓解这一限制，我们引入了动态开放网络环境中GUI代理的**主动文档引导操作**，这是一种新颖的范式，通过使代理能够自主搜索相关文档来解决长尾任务，模仿了人类的问题解决方式。为了评估代理在该范式中的能力，我们提出了**DocOS**，一个旨在完全交互环境中评估文档引导问题解决的基准。DocOS要求代理自主导航网络浏览器，定位相关的在线文档，理解程序性指令，并忠实地将它们落地为可执行的GUI操作。大量实验表明，进展受到双重瓶颈的严格约束：代理在主动搜索过程中难以可靠地定位相关信息，并且经常无法忠实地将检索到的指令落地为精确操作，这表明文档引导交互是使GUI代理在动态环境中实现自我进化的关键途径。

Original abstract: While Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents have shown promising performance in automated device interaction, they primarily depend on static parametric knowledge from pre-training or instruction tuning. This reliance fundamentally limits their ability to handle long-tailed tasks that require explicit procedural knowledge absent from model parameters, often forcing agents to resort to inefficient and brittle trial-and-error exploration. To mitigate this limitation, we introduce \textbf{Proactive Document-Guided Action} for GUI agents in dynamic, open-web environments, a novel paradigm that mirrors human problem-solving by enabling agents to autonomously search for relevant documentation to resolve long-tailed tasks. To evaluate agents' capability in this paradigm, we propose \textbf{DocOS}, a benchmark designed to assess document-guided problem solving in fully interactive environments. DocOS requires agents to autonomously navigate a web browser, locate relevant online documentation, comprehend procedural instructions, and faithfully ground them into executable GUI actions. Extensive experiments reveal that progress is strictly constrained by dual bottlenecks: agents struggle to reliably locate relevant information during proactive search and frequently fail to faithfully ground retrieved instructions into precise actions, pointing toward document-guided interaction as a crucial pathway for enabling self-evolving GUI agents in dynamic environments.

LMAC iteratively refines the protocol using an explicit state-awareness criterion, improving state recovery while narrowing differences in agents' knowledge. Experiments on diverse MARL benchmarks show that LMAC improves state reconstruction across agents and yields substantial performance gains over prior communication baselines.
